. 
. * Extract relevant variables, give intuitive names, code values as needed,
. * and combine files across states to generate cenXX.dta for each year
. do cen70code.do

. ******************************************************************************
. * cen70code.do
. * Dix-Carneiro and Kovak AER replication files
. *
. * Extract relevant variables from the 1970 Census, give intuitive names, 
. * code values as needed, and combine files across states to generate
. * cen70.dta.
. ******************************************************************************
. 
. foreach st in AC AL AM AP BA CE DF ES FN GB GO MA MG MT PA PB PE PI PR RJ ///
>               RN RO RR RS SC SE SP {
  2. 
.   use ./Census_Raw/1970/CENSO70_`st', clear
  3. 
.   gen xweighti = v054
  4. 
.   gen age = v027 if inlist(v026,3,4)
  5.   replace age = 0 if inlist(v026,1,2)
  6. 
.   gen female = (v023==1)
  7. 
.   * no race variable in 1970
. 
.   *** code IPUMS version of years of education based on available
.   *** variables
.   do cen70educ.do
  8. 
.   ** employment
.   gen employed = (v043==7)  // includes looking for work
  9.   replace employed = . if v043 >= .
 10.   
.   * no information on formality (either via carteira or previdencia)
.   
.   gen atividade1970 = v045 // same classification as 1991 but different codes
 11.   
.   gen ymain = v041 if v041 < 9999
 12.   
.   gen state = UF
 13. 
.   * cod70 has municipio code
. 
.   gen urbanrural = 1 if v004==0
 14.   replace urbanrural = 0 if inlist(v004,1,2)
 15.   
.   gen married = inrange(v040,1,3)
 16.   
.   gen othermunic5ya = 1 if inrange(v032,1,5)
 17.   replace othermunic5ya = 0 if inrange(v032,6,8)
 18. 
.   bysort id_dom num_fam: egen famsize = count(num_fam)
 19.   
.   gen inschool = (v043==1)
 20.   
.   keep xweighti age female educ employed atividade1970 ymain state ///
>        urbanrural married othermunic5ya famsize inschool cod70
 21.   
.   compress
 22.   save cen70code`st', replace
 23. }
(2449 missing values generated)
(2387 real changes made)

. foreach st in AC AL AM AP BA CE DF ES FN GB GO MA MG MT PA PB PE PI PR RJ ///
>               RN RO RR RS SC SE SP {
  2.   erase cen70code`st'.dta
  3. }

. 
end of do-file

. do cen80code.do

. ******************************************************************************
. * cen80code.do
. * Dix-Carneiro and Kovak AER replication files
. *
. * Extract relevant variables from the 1980 Census, give intuitive names, 
. * code values as needed, and combine files across states to generate
. * cen80.dta.
. ******************************************************************************
. 
. foreach st in 11 12 13 14 15 16 21 22 23 24 25 26 27 28 29 31a 31b 32 33a 33b 35a 35b 35c 41 42
>  43 50 51 52 53 {
  2. 
.   use ./Census_Raw/1980/cen80st`st', clear
  3. 
.   gen hhid = v601
  4.   bysort hhid: gen pernum = _n // no person number variable in survey
  5. 
.   gen xweighti = v604 // mean is 4.2 - corresponds to roughly 25% sample
  6. 
.   gen age = v606
  7.   replace age = . if v606 == 999
  8. 
.   gen female = (v501 == 3)
  9. 
.   gen race = .
 10.   replace race = 1 if v509 == 2 // branca
 11.   replace race = 2 if v509 == 8 // parda
 12.   replace race = 3 if v509 == 4 // preta
 13.   replace race = 4 if v509 == 6 // amarela
 14.   *** no code for indigena in 1980
.   
.   *** code IPUMS version of years of education based on available
.   *** variables
.   do cen80educ.do
 15.   
.   ** previdencia-based employment section (for comparison to 1991)
.   gen employed = (v528==1)
 16.   replace employed = . if v528 >= .
 17.                         // employed,      pays prev.           ag worker(1,2), employee
.   gen prev_formemp = 1 if (employed==1) & inlist(v534,2,4,6) & inlist(v533,1,2,6)
 18.   replace prev_formemp = 0 if prev_formemp!=1
 19.   gen prev_nonformemp = 1 if (employed==1) & (prev_formemp==0) // employed but not formally
 20.   replace prev_nonformemp = 0 if prev_nonformemp!=1
 21.                 //  not employed   looking for work (either worked before or not)
.   gen unemp = 1 if (employed!=1) & inlist(v529,1,2)
 22.   replace unemp = 0 if unemp!=1
 23.   gen nilf = 1 if (employed!=1) & (unemp!=1) // neither employed nor unemployed (i.e. not wo
> rking but not searching)
 24.   replace nilf = 0 if nilf!=1
 25.   **  
. 
.   ** alternate employment section
.   gen prev_anonformemp = 1 if (employed==1) & (prev_formemp==0) // employed but not formally
 26.   replace prev_anonformemp = 0 if prev_anonformemp!=1
 27.   replace prev_anonformemp = 0 if inlist(v533,8,9) // self employed, no answer
 28.   **  
. 
.   gen atividade = v532 // same codes as 1991
 29. 
.   gen ymain = v607 if v607 < 9999999
 30.   replace ymain = . if inlist(v607,9999999,.) // undeclared, unemployed
 31.   gen mw_ymain = ymain / 4150 // main earnings in multiples of minimum wage
 32.   
.   gen hmain_bin = v535 // binned into <15, 15-29, 30-39, 40-48, >=49
 33.   replace hmain_bin = . if v535 == 9
 34.   
.   gen yotherjob = v609 if v609 < 9999999
 35.   replace yotherjob = . if inlist(v609,9999999,.) // undeclared, unemployed
 36. 
.   gen halljob_bin = v536
 37. 
.   gen state = v002
 38.   gen mesoreg = state*100 + v003
 39.   gen microreg = state*1000 + v004
 40.   gen munic = state*10000 + v005
 41. 
.   gen urbanrural = v198 // city is coded as 1 (as in subsequent years)
 42.   
.   gen married = inrange(v526,1,3)
 43.   
.   * combine v518 (previous munic) with v517 (time in current munic)
.   gen munic5ya = v518 if inrange(v516,0,4) // was in differenc munic 5 years ago
 44.   replace munic5ya = munic if inrange(v516,5,8) // was still in current munic 5 years ago
 45.   replace munic5ya = . if v516 == 9
 46.   
.   * calculate family size using household id and family indicator (v505)
.   * v505 coding:
.   * - multiple household members, all in same family: 0
.   * - household contains only one individual: 5
.   * - household contains multiple individuals, belonging to multiple
.   *   families: 1, 2, or 3 indicating which family
.   * - group quarters: 4
.   bysort v601 v505: egen famsize = count(v505) if inrange(v505,0,3)
 47.   replace famsize = 1 if inrange(v505,4,5)
 48.   
.   gen inschool = inrange(v520,1,8) | inrange(v521,1,8) | inrange(v522,1,8)
 49.   
.   keep hhid pernum xweighti age female race educ employed prev_formemp prev_nonformemp ///
>        prev_anonformemp unemp nilf atividade ///
>        ymain hmain_bin yotherjob halljob_bin state mesoreg microreg munic urbanrural married //
> /
>            munic5ya famsize inschool mw_ymain
 50.   compress
 51.   save cen80code`st', replace
 52. }
(167 real changes made, 167 to missing)
(116536 missing values generated)

. do cen91code.do

. ******************************************************************************
. * cen91code.do
. * Dix-Carneiro and Kovak AER replication files
. *
. * Extract relevant variables from the 1991 Census, give intuitive names, 
. * code values as needed, and combine files across states to generate
. * cen91.dta.
. ******************************************************************************
. 
. foreach st in 11 12 13 14 15 16 17 21 22 23 24 25 26 27 28 29 31 32 33 35 36 41 42 43 50 51 52 
> 53 {
  2. 
.   use ./Census_Raw/1991/cen91st`st'com, clear
  3. 
.   gen long hhid = v102
  4.   gen pernum = v98
  5. 
.   gen xweighti = v7301 / (10^8)
  6. 
.   gen age = v3072
  7. 
.   gen female = (v301 == 2)
  8. 
.   gen race = .
  9.   replace race = 1 if v309 == 1 // branca
 10.   replace race = 2 if v309 == 4 // parda
 11.   replace race = 3 if v309 == 2 // preta
 12.   replace race = 4 if v309 == 3 // amarela
 13.   replace race = 5 if v309 == 5 // indigena
 14. 
.   gen educ = .
 15.   replace educ = 0 if inlist(v3241,0,30) // no instruction or adult literacy
 16.   replace educ = v3241 if inrange(v3241,1,17) // years of ed
 17.   replace educ = . if inlist(v3241,20,.) // undetermined or < 5 yrs old
 18. 
.   ** main employment section
.   gen employed = 1 if inlist(v345,1,2) // worked regularly or occassionally in last year
 19.   replace employed = 0 if employed!=1
 20.                   // employed,    has work card    ag worker, employee (private, public, sta
> te enterprise)
.   gen formemp = 1 if (employed==1) & (v350==1) & inlist(v349,1,6,7,8)
 21.   replace formemp = 0 if formemp!=1
 22.   gen nonformemp = 1 if (employed==1) & (formemp==0) // employed but not formally
 23.   replace nonformemp = 0 if nonformemp!=1
 24.                 //  not employed   looking for work (either worked before or not)
.   gen unemp = 1 if (employed!=1) & inlist(v358,1,2)
 25.   replace unemp = 0 if unemp!=1
 26.   gen nilf = 1 if (employed!=1) & (unemp!=1) // neither employed nor unemployed (i.e. not wo
> rking but not searching)
 27.   replace nilf = 0 if nilf!=1
 28.   **
. 
.   ** alternate employment section
.   gen anonformemp = 1 if (employed==1) & (formemp==0) // employed but not formally
 29.   replace anonformemp = 0 if anonformemp!=1
 30.   replace anonformemp = 0 if inlist(v349,9,11) // self employed, unpaid
 31.   **
.   
.   ** previdencia-based employment section (for comparison to 1980)
.                        // employed,       pays prev.  ag worker, employee (private, public, sta
> te enterprise)
.   gen prev_formemp = 1 if (employed==1) & (v353==1) & inlist(v349,1,6,7,8)
 32.   replace prev_formemp = 0 if prev_formemp!=1
 33.   gen prev_nonformemp = 1 if (employed==1) & (prev_formemp==0) // employed but not formally
 34.   replace prev_nonformemp = 0 if prev_nonformemp!=1
 35.   **
.   
.   ** alternate previdencia-based employment section
.   gen prev_anonformemp = 1 if (employed==1) & (prev_formemp==0) // employed but not formally
 36.   replace prev_anonformemp = 0 if prev_anonformemp!=1
 37.   replace prev_anonformemp = 0 if inlist(v349,9,11) // self employed, unpaid
 38.   **
.   
.   * auxiliary variables for informality study
.   gen selfemployed = (v349==9)
 39.   replace selfemployed = . if v349 >= .
 40.   gen workcard = (v350==1)
 41.   replace workcard = . if v350 >= .
 42. 
.   gen atividade = v347
 43. 
.   gen ymain = v356 if v356 < 9999999
 44.   replace ymain = . if inlist(v356,9999999,.) // undeclared, unemployed
 45.   gen mw_ymain = ymain / 36161.60
 46. 
.   gen hmain = v354
 47. 
.   gen yotherjob = v357 if v357 < 9999999
 48.   replace yotherjob = . if inlist(v357,9999999,.)
 49.   gen yalljob = ymain + yotherjob
 50.   drop yotherjob
 51.   
.   gen hotherjob = v355
 52.   gen halljob = hmain + hotherjob
 53.   drop hotherjob
 54. 
.   gen state = v1101
 55. 
.   gen mesoreg = state*100 + v7001
 56. 
.   gen microreg = state*1000 + v7002
 57. 
.   gen munic = state*10000 + v1102
 58. 
.   gen urbanrural = v1061
 59. 
.   gen married = inrange(v3342,1,3)
 60.   
.   gen munic5ya = v321*10000 + v3211 if inrange(v321,11,53) & inrange(v3211,1,7220) // valid sta
> te code and munic code
 61.   replace munic5ya = munic if v321 == 70 // in this municipio
 62.   replace munic5ya = munic if v314 == 1 // born in this municipio and always lived here (cau
> ses a skip over migration-related variables)
 63.   * implicitly coded as missing if reporting brazil, unspecified v321 == 54 
.   *                                foreign country v321 == 80
.   *                                state ignored v321 == 99
.   *                                municipio ignored or ill defined v3211 == 0
.   *                                people under age 5 v3211 == .
.   
.   gen famsize = v3041 + v3042
 64.   
.   gen inschool = inrange(v324,1,8) | inrange(v325,1,5) | inrange(v326,1,6)
 65.   
.   keep hhid pernum xweighti age female race educ employed formemp nonformemp prev_formemp prev_
> nonformemp ///
>        anonformemp prev_anonformemp unemp nilf atividade ymain hmain yalljob halljob state meso
> reg microreg ///
>            munic urbanrural married munic5ya famsize inschool ///
>            selfemployed workcard mw_ymain
 66.   compress
 67.   save cen91code`st', replace
 68. }

. use cen91code11, clear

. foreach st in 12 13 14 15 16 17 21 22 23 24 25 26 27 28 29 31 32 33 35 36 41 42 43 50 51 52 53 
> {
  2.   append using cen91code`st'
  3. }

. gen year = 1991

. compress
  year was float now int
  (34,091,310 bytes saved)

. save cen91, replace
file cen91.dta saved

. 
. foreach st in 11 12 13 14 15 16 17 21 22 23 24 25 26 27 28 29 31 32 33 35 36 41 42 43 50 51 52 
> 53 {
  2.   erase cen91code`st'.dta
  3. }

. 
end of do-file

. do cen00code.do

. ******************************************************************************
. * cen00code.do
. * Dix-Carneiro and Kovak AER replication files
. *
. * Extract relevant variables from the 2000 Census, give intuitive names, 
. * code values as needed, and combine files across states to generate
. * cen00.dta.
. ******************************************************************************
. 
. foreach st in 11 12 13 14 15 16 17 21 22 23 24 25 26 27 28 29 31 32 33 35 41 42 43 50 51 52 53 
> {
  2. 
.   use ./Census_Raw/2000/cen00st`st'com, clear
  3. 
.   gen hhid = v0300
  4.   gen pernum = v0400
  5. 
.   gen xweighti = p001
  6. 
.   gen age = v4752
  7. 
.   gen female = (v0401 == 2)
  8. 
.   gen race = .
  9.   replace race = 1 if v0408 == 1 // branca
 10.   replace race = 2 if v0408 == 4 // parda
 11.   replace race = 3 if v0408 == 2 // preta
 12.   replace race = 4 if v0408 == 3 // amarela
 13.   replace race = 5 if v0408 == 5 // indigena
 14. 
.   gen educ = .
 15.   replace educ = 0 if inlist(v4300,0,30) // no instruction or adult literacy
 16.   replace educ = v4300 if inrange(v4300,1,17) // years of ed
 17.   replace educ = . if inlist(v4300,20) // undetermined
 18. 
.   ** employment section
.   gen employed = 1 if v0439==1 | v0440==1 | v0441==1 | v0442==1 | v0443==1
 19.   replace employed = 0 if employed!=1
 20. 
.   gen formemp = 1 if (employed==1) & (v0447==3) // employed and employee (not domestic) with wo
> rk card
 21.   replace formemp = 0 if formemp!=1
 22. 
.   gen nonformemp = 1 if (employed==1) & (formemp==0) // employed but not formally
 23.   replace nonformemp = 0 if nonformemp!=1
 24. 
.                 //  not employed   looking for work
.   gen unemp = 1 if (employed!=1) & v0455==1
 25.   replace unemp = 0 if unemp!=1
 26. 
.   gen nilf = 1 if (employed!=1) & (unemp!=1) // neither employed nor unemployed (i.e. not worki
> ng but not searching)
 27.   replace nilf = 0 if nilf!=1
 28.   **  
. 
.   ** alternate employment section
.   gen anonformemp = 1 if (employed==1) & (formemp==0) // employed but not formally
 29.   replace anonformemp = 0 if anonformemp!=1
 30.   replace anonformemp = 0 if inlist(v0447,6,7,8,9) // self employed, apprentice, unpaid, own
>  consump
 31.   **  
.   
.   gen cnae = v4462
 32. 
.   gen ymain = v4512
 33.   gen mw_ymain = v4514 if ymain > 0 & ymain < .
 34. 
.   gen hmain = v0453
 35. 
.   gen yotherjob = v4522
 36.   gen yalljob = ymain + yotherjob
 37.   drop yotherjob
 38.   
.   gen hotherjob = v0454
 39.   gen halljob = hmain + hotherjob
 40.   drop hotherjob
 41. 
.   gen state = v0102
 42. 
.   gen mesoreg = v1002
 43. 
.   gen microreg = v1003
 44. 
.   gen munic = floor(v0103/10) // drop checksum digit
 45. 
.   gen urbanrural = v1005
 46. 
.   gen married = v0438 == 1
 47. 
.   gen munic5ya = floor(v4250/10) if inrange(v0424,3,4) // lived in a different municipio
 48.   replace munic5ya = . if (floor(v4250/10) - 10000*floor(v4250/100000)) == 0 // unspecified 
> municipio
 49.   replace munic5ya = munic if inrange(v0424,1,2) // lived in this municipio 5 yrs ago
 50.   replace munic5ya = munic if v0415 == 1 // always lived in this municipio (causes a skip ov
> er migration-related variables)
 51.   * implicitly coded as missing if foreign country or not born yet v0424 = 5,6
.   
.   * living outside state of birth
.   gen leftbirthst = .
 52.   replace leftbirthst = 0 if v0415 == 1 // never left birth municipio
 53.   replace leftbirthst = 0 if v0417 == 1 // lives in birth municipio (even if left at some po
> int)
 54.   replace leftbirthst = 0 if v0418 == 1 // born in current state
 55.   replace leftbirthst = 1 if leftbirthst != 0
 56.   replace leftbirthst = . if inlist(v0419,2,3) // omit non-native born
 57.   
.   * make famsize variable
.   * - v7401-v7406 tells the number of people in each family within a household
.   * - v7407-v7409 are all blank, since no family number is > 6
.   * - v0404 family number, tells which v740x to look at for that individual
.   gen famsize = .
 58.   replace famsize = v7401 if v0404==1
 59.   replace famsize = v7402 if v0404==2
 60.   replace famsize = v7403 if v0404==3
 61.   replace famsize = v7404 if v0404==4
 62.   replace famsize = v7405 if v0404==5
 63.   replace famsize = v7406 if v0404==6
 64.   
.   gen inschool = inrange(v0429,1,2)
 65.   
.   * commuting destination municipio
.   gen commutemunic = floor(v4276/10) // drop checksum digit.
 66.   replace commutemunic = . if mod(commutemunic,10000)==0 // if only report state set commute
>  munic to missing
 67.   replace commutemunic = . if v4276==0200006 // no work or school to commute to
 68.   replace commutemunic = munic if v4276==0100008 // works in this municipio
 69.   replace commutemunic = .a if floor(v4276/100000) >= 80 // works in other country
 70.   
.   keep hhid pernum xweighti age female race educ employed formemp nonformemp ///
>        anonformemp unemp nilf cnae ymain hmain yalljob halljob state mesoreg microreg ///
>            munic urbanrural married munic5ya famsize inschool commutemunic leftbirthst ///
>            mw_ymain
 71.   compress
 72.   save cen00code`st', replace
 73. }

. do cen10code.do

. ******************************************************************************
. * cen10code.do
. * Dix-Carneiro and Kovak AER replication files
. *
. * Extract relevant variables from the 2010 Census, give intuitive names, 
. * code values as needed, and combine files across states to generate
. * cen10.dta.
. ******************************************************************************
. 
. foreach st in AC AL AM AP BA CE DF ES GO MA MG MS MT PA PB PE PI PR RJ RN RO RR RS SC SE SP TO 
> {
  2.   use ./Census_Raw/2010/CENSO10_`st', clear
  3. 
.   gen hhid = v0300
  4.   destring hhid, replace
  5.   
.   gen pernum = v0504
  6.   
.   gen xweighti = v0010
  7. 
.   gen age = v6036
  8. 
.   gen female = (v0601 == 2)
  9. 
.   gen race = .
 10.   replace race = 1 if v0606 == 1 // branca
 11.   replace race = 2 if v0606 == 4 // parda
 12.   replace race = 3 if v0606 == 2 // preta
 13.   replace race = 4 if v0606 == 3 // amarela
 14.   replace race = 5 if v0606 == 5 // indigena
 15. 
.   do educ_censo_2010 // Years of education code from Guilherme Hirata (PUC-Rio)
 16.   rename anoest educ
 17. 
.   ** employment section
.   
.   gen employed = 1 if v0641==1 | v0642==1 | v0643==1 | v0644==1
 18.   replace employed = 0 if employed!=1
 19. 
.   gen formemp = 1 if (employed==1) & inlist(v0648,1,2,3) // employed and (employee with card, m
> ilitary, or civil svc.)
 20.   replace formemp = 0 if v0502==18 | inlist(v6461,5152,9111) // domestic workers (from house
> hold register, then occupations)
 21.   replace formemp = 0 if formemp!=1
 22. 
.   gen nonformemp = 1 if (employed==1) & (formemp==0) // employed but not formally
 23.   replace nonformemp = 0 if nonformemp!=1
 24.   
.                 //  not employed   looking for work
.   gen unemp = 1 if (employed!=1) & v0654==1
 25.   replace unemp = 0 if unemp!=1
 26. 
.   gen nilf = 1 if (employed!=1) & (unemp!=1) // neither employed nor unemployed (i.e. not worki
> ng but not searching)
 27.   replace nilf = 0 if nilf!=1
 28.   **  
.   
.   ** alternate employment section
.   gen anonformemp = 1 if (employed==1) & (formemp==0) // employed but not formally
 29.   replace anonformemp = 0 if anonformemp!=1  
 30.   replace anonformemp = 0 if inlist(v0648,5,7) // self employed, unpaid
 31.   **
.   
.   gen cnae = v6472 // retroactively compatible with Census 2000 (CNAE-Dom v1)
 32.   
.   gen ymain = v6511
 33.   gen mw_ymain = v6514 if ymain > 0 & ymain < .
 34. 
.   gen hmain = v0653
 35.   
.   gen yotherjob = v6521
 36.   gen yalljob = ymain + yotherjob
 37.   drop yotherjob
 38.   
.   gen hotherjob = . // no longer asked in 2010 Census
 39.   gen halljob = . // missing other job hours
 40. 
.   gen state = v0001
 41.   
.   destring v1002 v1003 v0002, replace
 42.   
.   gen mesoreg = 100*v0001 + v1002
 43.   
.   gen microreg = 1000*v0001 + v1003
 44.   
.   gen munic = 10000*v0001 + floor(v0002/10) // drop checksum digit
 45.   
.   gen urbanflag = (v1006==1)
 46.   
.   gen married = (v0640==1)
 47.   
.   gen munic5ya = floor(v6264/10) if v0626==1 // lived elsewhere in Brazil 5 years ago
 48.   replace munic5ya = munic if v0624>=6 // lived here for at least 6 years (causes a skip for
>  the munic 5ya question)
 49.   replace munic5ya = munic if v0618==1 // always lived here (causes a skip over migration-re
> lated variables)
 50.   * implicitly coded as missing if foreign country or not born yet
.   
.   gen famsize = .
 51.   replace famsize = v5060 if v5020 < . // gives direct family size measure in v5060
 52.   
.   gen inschool = inrange(v0628,1,2)
 53.   
.   * commuting
.   * v0660, v0662, and v0664
.   gen commutemunic = munic if inrange(v0660,1,2) // work in house or same munic
 54.   replace commutemunic = floor(v6604/10) if v0660==3 // work in other munic
 55.   replace commutemunic = . if inlist(v6604,8888888,9999999) & v0660==3 // munic not specifie
> d
 56.   replace commutemunic = .a if v0660==4 // other country
 57.   replace commutemunic = . if v0660==5 // multiple work locations, they don't ask munic
 58.   
.   keep hhid pernum xweighti age female race educ employed formemp nonformemp ///
>        anonformemp unemp nilf cnae ymain hmain yalljob halljob state mesoreg microreg ///
>            munic urbanflag married munic5ya famsize inschool commutemunic mw_ymain
 59.   compress
 60.   save cen10code`st', replace  
 61. }
hhid has all characters numeric; replaced as long
(93675 missing values generated)
(20913 real changes made)
(62858 real changes made)
(5277 real changes made)
(1807 real changes made)

. ******************************************************************************
. * code_sample_1970.do
. * Dix-Carneiro and Kovak AER replication files
. *
. * Generate Census 1970 variables for analysis and restrict sample
. ******************************************************************************
.

. * Sample restriction

. ***************************
. * Calculate wages and deflate
. 
. * Common currency and deflate prices (generates currency and defl)
. global baseyr = 2000

. global svyyrvar = "year"

. do census_deflators

. *******************************************************
. * census_deflators.do
. * Dix-Carneiro and Kovak AER replication files
. *
. * Generates price deflators for use with Census data
. *
. * Input: baseyr - global containing the survey year
. *                 that will serve as the base year
. *                 for the deflators.
. *        svyyrvar - global containing the name of the
. *                 variable defining the survey year
. *                 for each observation.
. *
. * Output: defl - variable containing the appropriate
. *                deflator for each observation.
. *******************************************************
. 
. local defl1960 = 0.000000000000007

. local defl1970 = 0.000000000000264

. local defl1980 = 0.000000000005748

. local defl1991 = 0.000067244146018

. local defl2000 = 0.890629059684618

. local defl2010 = 1.7385882995697 // calculated in inpc_ipeadata.xlsx

. 
. capture drop defl

. gen double defl = .
(11944766 missing values generated)

. 
. foreach yr in 1960 1970 1980 1991 2000 2010 {
  2.   replace defl = `defl`yr'' if $svyyrvar == `yr'
  3. }
(0 real changes made)
(11944766 real changes made)
(0 real changes made)
(0 real changes made)
(0 real changes made)
(0 real changes made)

.

end of do-file

. * Common currency and deflate prices (generates currency and defl)
. global baseyr = 2000

. global svyyrvar = "year"

. do census_deflators

. *******************************************************
. * census_deflators.do
. * Dix-Carneiro and Kovak AER replication files
. *
. * Generates price deflators for use with Census data
. *
. * Input: baseyr - global containing the survey year
. *                 that will serve as the base year
. *                 for the deflators.
. *        svyyrvar - global containing the name of the
. *                 variable defining the survey year
. *                 for each observation.
. *
. * Output: defl - variable containing the appropriate
. *                deflator for each observation.
. *******************************************************
. 
. local defl1960 = 0.000000000000007

. local defl1970 = 0.000000000000264

. local defl1980 = 0.000000000005748

. local defl1991 = 0.000067244146018

. local defl2000 = 0.890629059684618

. local defl2010 = 1.7385882995697 // calculated in inpc_ipeadata.xlsx

. 
. capture drop defl

. gen double defl = .
(15072917 missing values generated)

. 
. foreach yr in 1960 1970 1980 1991 2000 2010 {
  2.   replace defl = `defl`yr'' if $svyyrvar == `yr'
  3. }
(0 real changes made)
(0 real changes made)
(15072917 real changes made)
(0 real changes made)
(0 real changes made)
(0 real changes made)

. 
. replace defl = defl / `defl$baseyr'
(15072917 real changes made)

. 
end of do-file

. do census_currency

. *******************************************************
. * census_currency.do
. * Dix-Carneiro and Kovak AER replication files
. *
. * Generates currency adjustment values for use with 
. * Census data.
. *
. * Output: currency - variable with currency adjustments
. *******************************************************
. 
. capture drop currency

. gen double currency = .
(15072917 missing values generated)

. 
. replace currency = 2750000000000 if year == 1960
(0 real changes made)

. replace currency = 2750000000000 if year == 1970
(0 real changes made)

. replace currency = 2750000000000 if year == 1980
(15072917 real changes made)

. replace currency = 2750000       if year == 1991
(0 real changes made)

. replace currency = 1             if year == 2000
(0 real changes made)

. replace currency = 1             if year == 2010
(0 real changes made)

. 
. 
end of do-file

. do code_sample.do

. ******************************************************************************
. * code_sample_1970.do
. * Dix-Carneiro and Kovak AER replication files
. *
. * Generate Census 1991, 2000, and 2010 variables for analysis and restrict
. * sample
. ******************************************************************************
. 
. ***************************
. * Read in data and restrict sample
. 
. use cen91, clear

. append using cen00
(note: variable hhid was long, now double to accommodate using data's values)

. append using cen10
(note: variable hmain was byte, now int to accommodate using data's values)

. compress
  hhid was double now long
  (231,822,156 bytes saved)

. 
. ***************************
. * Sample restriction
. 
. keep if inrange(age,18,64)
(24528596 observations deleted)

. 
. ***************************
. * Calculate wages and deflate
. 
. * Calculate wages (generates wageall and wagemain)
. gen wageall = (yalljob/4.33)/halljob
(27695772 missing values generated)

. gen wagemain = (ymain/4.33)/hmain
(13456949 missing values generated)

. 
. * Common currency and deflate prices (generates currency and defl)
. global baseyr = 2000

. global svyyrvar = "year"

. do census_deflators

. *******************************************************
. * census_deflators.do
. * Dix-Carneiro and Kovak AER replication files
. *
. * Generates price deflators for use with Census data
. *
. * Input: baseyr - global containing the survey year
. *                 that will serve as the base year
. *                 for the deflators.
. *        svyyrvar - global containing the name of the
. *                 variable defining the survey year
. *                 for each observation.
. *
. * Output: defl - variable containing the appropriate
. *                deflator for each observation.
. *******************************************************
. 
. local defl1960 = 0.000000000000007

. local defl1970 = 0.000000000000264

. local defl1980 = 0.000000000005748

. local defl1991 = 0.000067244146018

. local defl2000 = 0.890629059684618

. local defl2010 = 1.7385882995697 // calculated in inpc_ipeadata.xlsx

. 
. capture drop defl

. gen double defl = .
(33426943 missing values generated)

. 
. foreach yr in 1960 1970 1980 1991 2000 2010 {
  2.   replace defl = `defl`yr'' if $svyyrvar == `yr'
  3. }
(0 real changes made)
(0 real changes made)
(0 real changes made)
(9070475 real changes made)
(11603690 real changes made)
(12752778 real changes made)

. 
. replace defl = defl / `defl$baseyr'
(33426943 real changes made)

. 
end of do-file

.

. * Generate rent variables for Moretti price index analysis
. do rent91code.do

. ******************************************************************************
. * rent91code.do
. * Dix-Carneiro and Kovak AER replication files
. *
. * Extract relevant variables from the 1991 Census for Moretti (2013) price
. * index analysis.
. ******************************************************************************
. 
. foreach st in 11 12 13 14 15 16 17 21 22 23 24 25 26 27 28 29 31 32 33 35 36 41 42 43 50 51 52 
> 53 {
  2. 
.   use ./Census_Raw/1991/cen91st`st', clear
  3. 
.   gen year = 1991
  4.   keep if v99==1 // household records only
  5.   gen long hhid = v102 // household ID
  6.   gen xweighth = v7300 / (10^8) // household weight
  7. 
.   * restrict sample to renters in permanent structures
.   keep if v208==3 // renting
  8.   keep if v201==1 // permanent structure
  9.   
.   * geography
.   gen state = v1101
 10.   gen mesoreg = state*100 + v7001
 11.   gen microreg = state*1000 + v7002
 12.   gen munic = state*10000 + v1102
 13.   
.   * monthly rent (nominal)
.   gen rent = v209
 14.   replace rent = . if inlist(rent,0,999999)
 15. 
.   * features
.   gen urban = inlist(v1061,1,2,3)
 16.   
.   gen walls = 1 if v203==1 // masonry (alvenaria)
 17.   replace walls = 2 if v203==2 // timber (madeira aparelhada)
 18.   replace walls = 3 if v203==3 // bare mud (taipa no revestida)
 19.   replace walls = 4 if v203==4 // improvised materials (material aproveitado)
 20.   replace walls = 5 if v203==5 // straw (palha)
 21.   replace walls = 6 if v203==6 // other
 22.   
.   gen rooms = v211 // number of rooms
 23.   gen bedrooms = v212 // number of bedrooms
 24.   gen bathrooms = v213 // number of bathrooms
 25.   
.   gen sewer = 0 if v206==0 // none
 26.   replace sewer = 1 if v206==1 // modern sewer system
 27.   replace sewer = 2 if inlist(v206,2,3) // septic tank (connected to sewer or not)
 28.   replace sewer = 3 if v206==4 // rustic pit
 29.   replace sewer = 4 if v206==5 // trench
 30.   replace sewer = 5 if v206==6 // other 
 31. 
.   gen public_water = inlist(v205,1,4)
 32.   
.   keep year hhid xweighth state mesoreg microreg munic rent urban walls ///
>        rooms bedrooms bathrooms sewer public_water
 33.   compress
 34.   save rent91code`st', replace
 35. }

. do rent10code.do

. ******************************************************************************
. * rent10code.do
. * Dix-Carneiro and Kovak AER replication files
. *
. * Extract relevant variables from the 2010 Census for Moretti (2013) price
. * index analysis.
. ******************************************************************************
. 
. *************************
. * Get household only extract from 2010 Census
. 
. foreach st in AC AL AM AP BA CE DF ES GO MA MG MS MT PA PB PE PI PR RJ RN RO RR RS SC SE SP TO 
> {
  2. 
.   use ./Census_Raw/2010/CENSO10_`st', clear
  3. 
.   * keep only household variables
.   keep v0001 v0002 v0011 v0300 v0010 v1001 v1002 v1003 v1004 v1006 v4001 ///
>        v4002 v0201 v2011 v2012 v0202 v0203 v6203 v0204 v6204 v0205 v0206 /// 
>            v0207 v0208 v0209 v0210 v0211 v0212 v0213 v0214 v0215 v0216 v0217 ///
>            v0218 v0219 v0220 v0221 v0222 v0301 v0401 v0402 v0701 v6529 v6530 ///
>            v6531 v6532 v6600 v6210 
  4.   duplicates drop
  5. 
.   gen year = 2010
  6.   gen xweighth = v0010
  7.   
.   * restrict sample to renters in permanent structures
.   keep if v0201==3 // renting
  8.   keep if v4001==1 // permanent structure
  9. 
.   * geography
.   gen state = v0001
 10.   destring v1002 v1003 v0002, replace
 11.   gen mesoreg = 100*v0001 + v1002
 12.   gen microreg = 1000*v0001 + v1003
 13.   gen munic = 10000*v0001 + floor(v0002/10) // drop checksum digit
 14. 
.   * monthly rent (nominal)
.   gen rent = v2011
 15.   
.   * features
.   gen urban = (v1006==1)
 16.   
.   gen walls = 1 if inlist(v0202,1,2) // masonry (alvenaria)
 17.   replace walls = 2 if v0202==3 // timber (madeira apraelhada)
 18.   replace walls = 3 if v0202==5 // bare mud (taipa no revestida)
 19.   replace walls = 4 if v0202==6 // improvised materials (material aproveitado)
 20.   replace walls = 5 if v0202==7 // straw (palha)
 21.   replace walls = 5 if inlist(v0202,4,8) // other
 22.   
.   gen rooms = v0203 // number of rooms
 23.   gen bedrooms = v0204 // number of bedrooms
 24.   gen bathrooms = v0205 // number of bathrooms
 25. 
.   gen sewer = 0 if v0206==2 // none
 26.   replace sewer = 1 if v0207==1 // modern sewer system
 27.   replace sewer = 2 if v0207==2 // septic tank
 28.   replace sewer = 3 if v0207==3 // rustic pit
 29.   replace sewer = 4 if v0207==4 // trench
 30.   replace sewer = 5 if inlist(v0207,5,6) // river,lake,sea, other
 31.   
.   gen public_water = v0208==1
 32.   
.   keep year xweighth state mesoreg microreg munic rent urban walls ///
>        rooms bedrooms bathrooms sewer public_water
 33.   compress
 34.   save rent10code`st', replace
 35. }

. use rent10codeAC, clear

. foreach st in AL AM AP BA CE DF ES GO MA MG MS MT PA PB PE PI PR RJ RN RO RR RS SC SE SP TO {
  2.   append using rent10code`st'
  3. }
(note: variable microreg was int, now float to accommodate using data's values)
(note: variable rent was int, now float to accommodate using data's values)

. compress
  (0 bytes saved)

. save rent10, replace
file rent10.dta saved

. 
. 
. foreach st in AC AL AM AP BA CE DF ES GO MA MG MS MT PA PB PE PI PR RJ RN RO RR RS SC SE SP TO 
> {
  2.   erase rent10code`st'.dta
  3. }

. 
. 
. 
end of do-file
